3/ The total of the taxes herein corresponds to the total of the taxes on copper and sugar in the Miscellaneous column in the preceding table, plus all taxes included in appropriate tariff schedules.
4/ Figures are rounded to nearest dollar, and will not necessarily add to totals.

14

Cash Income and Outgo of the Treasury
